The hotel is about 100 meters away from the river, so it is quiet and convenient. There is no doubt about this.
2. Service: After getting off the bus from the north gate, the hotel staff will come to help take some of the luggage and lead the way. This is the normal level of the local hotel. Other hotels did not provide basic information, such as what facilities are available in the hotel and what activities are suitable for taking photos of internet celebrities, but they were not introduced on the way to the room. The next day, the little girl at the front desk gave me a bottle of rice wine. Although I told him the wrong person, I insisted on giving it to me after learning the truth. This seemed generous and decent.
3. Facilities: The hotel is in the style of a homestay, an old stilted building. I will not use it to match the five-star hotel, but at least maintenance should be done. The downlights flashing in the corridor and an empty space above the tatami The lamp holder, as well as the lamp ***** plug that fell off the washbasin, seemed lack of maintenance. This season is humid, hotels of this grade should still be equipped with dehumidifiers, because the temperature in Xijiang is not too high, children with air-conditioning or people with weak physical conditions may feel cold, but they will feel damp if they do not open the bedding and the room. There are many mosquitoes in the room. It is understandable that there are no screen windows in the antique building on the stilts, but the mosquito-killing supplies are not placed in advance in the southern summer, and you need to contact the front desk to send them.
4. Hygiene: The lid of the kettle looks dirty, there is a small blood stain on the bed sheet that has been cleaned but not completely washed off, there is a spider web standing on the bed, there is a spider in the corner above the bedside table, sleeping at night Another spider fell on my wife and was knocked out. The spider that fell on her body is understandable. After all, it is the stilted building in the lofty mountains of Miao Village and it cannot be completely enclosed. But as mentioned earlier, the four places should be solved when the room is cleaned and linen, shouldn't they show up?
The overall feeling is that I can understand if it is a hotel or homestay in a scenic area within a thousand that can achieve this level, but the price of more than 2,600 high-end homestay hotels, and the type of hotel ranked sixth by Ctrip, disappoints me. This type There are not many hotel rooms, unlike the hundreds of guest rooms in major hotels, the selling point should be exquisite service. Although the room is a stilt building, the selling point should be a clean and tidy environment. As a user of Ctrip for the past ten years, I can't help asking whether Ctrip has continued to follow up after ranking hotels?
